Title: Re: Anybody interested in LSD Gummy Stars?
Post by: mambosun on November 25, 2011, 03:07 am
Have everyone who's sampling send you their address encrypted with your PGP in a PM.  Send the samples in a plain white envelope with printed address labels.  You want your envelopes to blend in with the business mail that USPS is sorting on a daily basis.

Since you're sending LSD I really can't imagine you having any problems.  Try to keep you packages simple and you should be golden.

Title: Re: *FREE SAMPLES* Anybody interested in LSD Gummy Stars?
Post by: FinnMacCool on December 04, 2011, 06:24 pm
Maybe its just the psychonaut in me, but I tend to think the best of people. That said Im newish here so take this for what you will.
Firstoff, GummyStars doesnt seem to be acting in the same manner that other scammers on this site have (reading past forum discussions).
He's been very responsive to PMs and on the boards. Not just once his sale went up either - he spent basically a week on here prior to sales speaking with experienced sellers to figure out the correct procedures to use.
He hasnt asked anyone to finalize early, just offered it for a little quid pro quo. I think wanting to keep your stash re-upped is a pretty normal thing, and beside the possibility of a scam, this is a pretty damn smart initial business strategy - as can be seen by the drought in the sales of some reputable sellers.
As someone said earlier, it would be high time for him to have bounced already if scamming. I would imagine that by this point anyone on the fence is probably staying there until some of these samples arrive, so he really wouldnt have much to gain by sticking around on the boards and calmly urging patience - as he has done.
He isn't shipping outside the U.S. In my mind if you were simply here for a week or whatever to scam people why would you limit your profits by not accepting orders? especially since international orders would take even longer for shipping to arrive, thus elongating the scamming window of opportunity. Same concept applies in reverse, if he was scamming, why not say he was in Germany or something so that the amount of time before he was found out would be almost doubled.
When you take all this stuff together, it just doesnt form a legitimate pattern of activity that I think someone interested in simply robbing money from others would follow.

Basically, Im a little nervous, as like I said, Im kindof new to this, but if GummyStars is a scammer he is the fucking Professor Moriarty of SilkRoad and I've just been taken to school.

But like I said, this is basically my first time in this rodeo, so take all this with a grain of salt.

Cheers! everybody, and I hope in a week we will all be reflecting on how awesome those gummy stars turned out to be!

Title: Re: *FREE SAMPLES* Anybody interested in LSD Gummy Stars?
Post by: MagicMan on December 07, 2011, 07:02 pm
This has got to be one of the most intense dramatic events that I have ever seen unfold on SR. As for what happened, I have to agree with a slightly modified "slutwalk" logic, we should teach not-to-scam at least as much as not-to-get-scammed. Right now there are no disincentives to scam people on here, sure people will bitch and moan and yell and threaten, but that, in my months on here, has never done anything to reverse or fix the scam.

We need to, as a community, provide the disincentive necessary to stop scammers. An example must be made of a scammer who we are certain is a scammer beyond a reasonable doubt. We must also, however, be careful not to provide these disincentives to people who made honest mistakes. The hardest part of all this is finding the line between the two in this kind of charged environment.

Title: Re: *FREE SAMPLES* Anybody interested in LSD Gummy Stars?
Post by: FinnMacCool on December 08, 2011, 06:35 pm
DBone,

Sorry man but your quite wrong about this. Gummy candies can easily be used as a means of conveyance for LSD. I have actually eaten several bears with liquid dropped onto them. A simple google search before posting would have cleared this up for you. Next time do a bit of research before immediately jumping to conjecture.

1. Gummy candies actually soak up most liquids quite well. For example, I know people who soak gummy bears in vodka, and they normally swell up to about twice their original size, and do not "leak" any of the liquid out in transportation, eating, etc. Haha they can actually get you pretty fucked up.
2. Most liquid is an alcohol suspension of the LSD. Even if the acid wouldnt soak in as you claim, the alcohol would evaporate very quickly from the surface, and leave a surface residue of LSD.
3. Like Mambo said, I think he makes these himself anyway, negating your whole argument.

I can only assume that the sheer novelty of the idea made people want to jump on it.  Or the lower prices.  But why would it be cheaper to dose gummy stars with LSD (however the fuck that would even work, I dunno), than to dose blotter paper?  There are so many holes in that idea I don't even know where to start!

But all that aside, yeah, his behavior alone should have been enough to out him as a scam.  Even if he'd been selling blotter acid, offering an absurd, unprofitable deal to people who finalize early should be an immediate red flag, I think?
Title: Re: *FREE SAMPLES* Anybody interested in LSD Gummy Stars?
Post by: ksoze on February 11, 2012, 06:40 am
As someone who got scammed by gummy stars, I bought them for a few reasons:

1.  They were promoted as having a higher than average dose than a typical blotter. 
2.  At the time, GummyStars was also one of the few (only?  I can't remember) US-based vendors. I'd been burned previously by attempting to buy LSD blotter from a reputable dutch vendor.  The blotter never arrived (I believe it was seized).
3.  They were inexpensive (given the dose).
4.  LSD in gelatin form is less exposed to air/light, which means it will degrade at a lower rate.
5.  Gummy stars look like candy.  Barry Cooper (former police officer, produced "Never Get Busted" video) said that he had never busted someone for drugs in the form of an edible.
